## 1. Event Dates and Overall Schedule Structure

### Event Dates
- **Sunday, April 19, 2026** - Pre-conference day (12 sessions)
- **Monday, April 20, 2026** - Main conference day 1 (105 sessions)
- **Tuesday, April 21, 2026** - Main conference day 2 (124 sessions)
- **Wednesday, April 22, 2026** - Final conference day (75 sessions)
- **TBD / No date assigned** - 9 sessions
